***разъехаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разъехаться.html>разъе́хаться</a> (10870)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jéxatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go (by vehicle)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разъехаться.html>разъе́хаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razʺjéxatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разъезжаться.html>разъезжа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to depart, to leave</li>
<li>to disperse</li>
<li>to pass by one another <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">on a narrow road, etc.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to pass by and miss one another, to fail to meet</li>
<li>to separate, to break up <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of a couple</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall apart</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разъяривший.html>разъяри́вший</a> (9773)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разъяривший.html>разъяри́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razʺjarívšij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разъяснение.html>разъясне́ние</a> (10352)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разъяснить.html>разъясни́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razʺjasnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разъяснение.html>разъясне́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razʺjasnénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разъяснение.html>разъясне́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разъяснение.html>разъясне́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разъяснение.html>разъясне́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>clarification, explanation, elucidation, interpretation</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разъяснить.html>разъясни́ть</a> (7879)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разъяснить.html>разъясни́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razʺjasnítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разъяснять.html>разъясня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to explain, to interpret
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разъяснить.html>разъясни́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:задача.html>зада́чу</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова</a>)</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razʺjasnítʹ</b> komú-libo zadáču (značénije slova)</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">explain the problem (the meaning of the word) to someone</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***разъяснявший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разъяснять.html>разъясня́вший</a> (11959)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разъяснять.html>разъясня́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razʺjasnjávšij</span>)
</p>

***разъяснять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разъяснять.html>разъясня́ть</a> (11959)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разъяснять.html>разъясня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razʺjasnjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разъяснить.html>разъясни́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to explain, to interpret
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разъяснять.html>разъясня́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:задача.html>зада́чу</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова</a>)</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razʺjasnjátʹ</b> komú-libo zadáču (značénije slova)</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">explain the problem (the meaning of the word) to somebody</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">igrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разыграть.html>разыгра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razygrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разыгрывать.html>разы́грывать</a></b>)

***разыграться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разыграться.html>разыгра́ться</a> (12516)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разыграть.html>разыгра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razygrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разыграться.html>разыгра́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razygrátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разыгрываться.html>разы́грываться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become frolicsome</li>
<li><i>(pianist, actor etc)</i> to warm up</li>
<li><i>(wind, sea etc)</i> to rise, to break</li>
<li>to run high
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разыграться.html>разыгра́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мигрень.html>мигре́нь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>razygrálasʹ</b> migrénʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his migraine broke out [make itself felt]; he had an attack of headache</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разыграться.html>разыгра́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:аппетит.html>аппети́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>razygrálsja</b> appetít</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he felt hungry; he developed an appetite; his appetite grew</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разыграться.html>разыгра́лось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воображение.html>воображе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>razygrálosʹ</b> voobražénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his imagination has broken loose</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to unfold, to develop, to take place
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разыграться.html>разыгра́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:драма.html>дра́ма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tam <b>razygrálasʹ</b> nastojáščaja dráma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a true drama unfolded [took place] there</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разыграться.html>разыгра́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скандал.html>сканда́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razygrálsja</b> skandál</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a scandal arose</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разыграть.html>разыгра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razygrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разыгрывать.html>разы́грывать</a> (8206)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разыграть.html>разыгра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razygrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разыгрывать.html>разы́грывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razýgryvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разыграть.html>разыгра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to play, to perform
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разыгрывать.html>разы́грывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурак.html>дура́ка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razýgryvatʹ</b> duráka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to play the fool, make a fool of oneself</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разыгрывать.html>разы́грывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сцена.html>сце́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razýgryvatʹ</b> scénu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put up an act</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to raffle off, to draw</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to play a trick, to play a practical joke, to pull one's leg</li></ol>

***разыгрываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разыгрываться.html>разы́грываться</a> (18298)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разыгрывать.html>разы́грывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razýgryvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разыгрываться.html>разы́грываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razýgryvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разыграться.html>разыгра́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become frolicsome</li>
<li><i>(pianist, actor etc)</i> to warm up</li>
<li><i>(wind, sea etc)</i> to rise, to break</li>
<li>to run high</li>
<li>to unfold, to develop, to take place</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разыгрывать.html>разы́грывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razýgryvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разыскивать.html>разы́скивавший</a> (6126)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***рай.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рай.html>рай</a> (3099)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rajь</i>, borrowed from Iranian, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Iranian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Iranian language">Proto-Iranian</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ira-pro">*RaHíš</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-Iranian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-Iranian language">Proto-Indo-Iranian</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="iir-pro">*RaHíš</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*reh₁ís</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wealth, goods</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:районный.html>райо́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:исполнительный.html>исполни́тельный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комитет.html>комите́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rajónnyj ispolnítelʹnyj komitét</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">district executive committee</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:районный.html>райо́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комитет.html>комите́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rajónnyj komitét</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:райком.html>райко́м</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rajkóm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:райком.html>райко́ма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:райком.html>райко́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:райком.html>райко́мов</a></b>)

***район.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:район.html>район</a> (787)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1865. Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">rayon</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">rai</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">-on</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">radius</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:район.html>райо́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rajón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:район.html>райо́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:район.html>райо́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:район.html>райо́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>district</li>
<li>region, area</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:районный.html>райо́нный</a> (4195)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:район.html>райо́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rajón</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:районный.html>райо́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rajónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> district; regional
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:районный.html>райо́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:центр.html>центр</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rajónnyj</b> centr</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>district</b> centre</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***рак.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рака.html>рак</a> (8283)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rakъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рака.html>рак</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rak</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рака.html>ра́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рака.html>ра́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рак.html>ра́ков</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рачий.html>ра́чий</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раковый.html>ра́ковый</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">рачо́к</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>crawfish, crayfish
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хал</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грек.html>гре́ка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>ре́ку</a>,<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́дит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грек.html>гре́ка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>ре́ке</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рака.html>ра́к</a></b>,<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:сунуть.html>су́нул</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грек.html>гре́ка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>ре́ку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a>,<br /><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рака.html>ра́к</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грек.html>гре́ку</a> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:цап.html>ца́п</a></i>!</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Russian tongue twister</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jéxal Gréka čerez réku,<br />vídit Gréka v réke <b>rák</b>,<br />súnul Gréka v réku rúku,<br /><b>rák</b> za rúku Gréku — <i>cáp</i>!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Across the river Greka rode,<br />In the river Greka sees a <b>crawdad</b>,<br />In the river Greka stuck his hand,<br />At Greka's hand the <b>crawdad</b> goes snap!</span></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>

***рака.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рака.html>ра́ка</a> (7005)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:рака.html>ра́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">monument, shrine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:рака.html>ра́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ráka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">casket with relics</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ра̏ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grave crypt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">ráka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crypt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌰𐍂𐌺𐌰</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">arka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chest, coffer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">arca</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chest, coffer, coffin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; or directly from the Latin. Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раковина.html>ра́ковина</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rákovina</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orky</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (genitive <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*orkъve</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*arkō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chest, coffer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">arca</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chest, coffer, coffin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> as above.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рака.html>ра́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ráka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рака.html>ра́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рака.html>ра́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рака.html>рак</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shrine <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a massive tomb holding the relics of a saint’s body</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ракета.html>раке́та</a> (1955)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ракета.html>раке́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rakéta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ракета.html>раке́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ракета.html>раке́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ракета.html>раке́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rocket (vehicle propelled by a rocket engine)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ракета.html>раке́та</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:запущенный.html>запу́щена</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:орбита.html>орби́ту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:опоздание.html>опозда́нием</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Rakéta</b> bylá zapúščena na orbítu s opozdánijem.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>The rocket</b> was launched into the orbit with a delay.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>missile
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">Самолёт <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбитый.html>сбит</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ракета.html>раке́той</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:класс.html>кла́сса</a> земля́-во́здух.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Samoljót byl sbit <b>rakétoj</b> klássa zemljá-vózdux.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The plane was shot down with the surface-to-air missile.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
